- Decision ID: DEC-0075
- Requested By: Owner-scheduled (2026-07-14): the deferred backlog **D4** VDP-timing-depth work — the CPU↔command-engine VRAM access-slot CONTENTION model — is the next milestone, following the DEC-0074 note that v1.1.4 landed only the CONTAINED per-command cost corrections and explicitly left the full slot-contention model DEFERRED.
- Approved By: MSX Master Agent (coordinator). Opens **M48** in the PLANNING phase (planner-first). Universal, spec-modeling fixes only (never game-specific), under the reference-precedence directive (DEC-0073).
- Decision: **Open M48 — V9958 command-engine ↔ CPU VRAM access-slot CONTENTION model, ban-respecting + formula-based.** Planner package: `docs/m48-planner-package.md`.
  - **What M48 adds** (as a pure timing/STATUS overlay on the existing S#2 CE/TR busy windows; VRAM mutation stays ATOMIC, M44 render-sync untouched): **Slice 1** — a per-line command-throughput cap from the three tier-1 fact-sheet §8 slot COUNTS (154 display-off / 88 sprites-off / 31 sprites-on), sprite-aware, superseding the DEC-0069 empirical `kActiveDisplaySlotFactorPercent` (200/300%) placeholder; **Slice 2** — CPU-concurrent-access command slowdown (CPU-priority: each CPU `#98` VRAM access during a busy command steals one slot ≈ `ceil(1368/S/6)` T-states, extending the command's CE window; the CPU access itself is NEVER stalled/delayed/dropped ⇒ CPU timing byte-identical).
  - **HARD BAN (non-negotiable — `feedback_license_sensitive_scope.md`, guardrails license-isolation, CLAUDE.md C1/D4, re-affirmed DEC-0074):** the openMSX `references/openmsx-21.0/src/video/VDPAccessSlots.cc:14-141` ~340-entry per-slot POSITION tables are BANNED — read for EFFECT only, NEVER transcribed/re-derived/curve-fit into `src/` under any name. The ONLY legal numeric inputs are 154/88/31, 1368, 6 (a 3-valued lookup + an average-rate formula, NOT a per-slot position array). If faithfulness would REQUIRE the banned table, the honest disposition is the average-throughput approximation (planner package §7), not smuggling.
  - **Tier-1 grounding (DEC-0073):** `references/fact-sheets/Yamaha V9958 VDP.md` §8 line 163 (three slot counts + CPU-priority slot-steal + "HMMV cut ~2× by simultaneous `OUT (#98),A`" + line-by-line), §7 line 124 (1368 VDP cyc/line), §1 line 34 / §7 line 129 (HB-F1XV does NOT wire the V9958 /WAIT → the command→CPU stall direction is out of scope on tier-1 hardware grounds), §6 line 120 (sprites slow commands identically whenever enabled, independent of count).
  - **What CANNOT be done within the ban (honest ceiling):** the cycle-exact per-slot model (exact VDP-cycle each access lands, exact 31-slot gap structure, cycle-exact too-fast dropped-request, raster-position command/CPU tearing) needs the banned position table → stays UNBUILDABLE-WITHOUT-FABRICATION (C1/D4 remainder, unchanged). "Parity" for M48 = aggregate CE/TR busy-window timing matching the fact-sheet §8 slot model ON AVERAGE (correct direction + rough magnitude of the sprites-on and CPU-concurrent slowdown), with pixel output bit-exact (13 modes 0.000%) and CPU timing bit-exact.
  - **Evidence gates:** build (both exes) + full ctest (228/228 + new oracles); **full ZEXALL/ZEXDOC sweep MANDATORY at QA** (the `feedback_slow_test_cadence.md` withhold-substitute shortcut is NOT taken this milestone — the CPU↔VRAM access-gating path is touched, even though `src/devices/cpu`/`src/core` diffs are expected EMPTY); all 13 M41 screen modes still 0.000% vs openMSX; a command-engine timing A/B (3 slot states + concurrent-`OUT`); non-tautology (oracles re-derived from tier-1, adversarial mutation fails, no existing oracle weakened); ban attestation (QA greps `src/`).
  - **Risks (all real, per planner package §6):** R1 CPU-timing shift (mitigation: no CPU stall/drop + AC-4 empty diff + EG-5 ZEXALL); R2 atomic-write/M44 coexistence (timing/STATUS-only overlay); R3 HIGH all-games blast radius (full 13-mode A/B + command-timing A/B + owner live spot-check of DEC-0069 titles; normal human-release gate, no auto-close); R4 determinism / `--vdp-cmd-bias` default-0 preserved.
- Impacted Milestones: **M48 (opens, PLANNING).** Expected edits confined to `src/devices/video/` (`vdp_access_timing.h` + `v9958_vdp.*`); ZERO `src/core`, ZERO `src/devices/cpu`. Backlog D4/C1: the average-throughput CONTENTION model is a ban-respecting PARTIAL close; the cycle-exact per-slot remainder stays OPEN/UNBUILDABLE-WITHOUT-FABRICATION. No new backlog rows.
- Effective Date: 2026-07-14

- Decision ID: DEC-0076
- Requested By: Owner-scheduled / coordinator (2026-07-14): the deferred backlog **D9** VDP sprite-fidelity work — per-line LIVE sprite attribute/register fetch — is the next scheduled milestone, following a completed cross-validated investigation that root-caused the Space Manbow / Laydock 2 top-region sprite culling + flicker to a single architectural defect (the sprite subsystem is FRAME-ATOMIC while the background is per-line-live).
- Approved By: MSX Master Agent (coordinator). Opens **M49** in the PLANNING phase (planner-first). Universal, spec-modeling fix only (never game-specific), under the reference-precedence directive (DEC-0073).
- Decision: **Open M49 — per-line LIVE sprite attribute/register fetch, closing backlog D9.** Planner package: `docs/m49-planner-package.md`.
  - **Confirmed root cause (tier-1 grounded):** `SpriteEngine::recompute_frame()` (`src/devices/video/sprite_engine.cpp:74-301`) is called ONLY from `V9958Vdp::on_vsync()` (`src/devices/video/v9958_vdp.cpp:685-705`), snapshotting the whole `control_regs` file + all VRAM at end-of-frame and computing every output line's visibility / 5th-sprite / position at once. Registers baked frame-final: R#23 vscroll (`:138`,`:183`), R#8 SPD+TP (`:103-105`,`:247`), R#1 BL/SI/MAG (`:102`,`:108-110`), R#5/R#11 attr base (`:116-117`,`:132`), R#6 pattern base (`:136`). The BACKGROUND is per-line-live via the M32 seam `Hbf1xvMachine::VdpRenderSyncAdapter::on_before_state_change()` (`src/machine/hbf1xv_machine.cpp:53-124`, +2-line margin `:101`). Space Manbow + Laydock 2 do CYCLE-TIMED mid-frame VDP reprogramming (NOT line interrupts: R#0 IE1=0, R#19=0xDB) to split a fixed HUD over a scrolling playfield; the end-of-frame snapshot captures the bottom/playfield state → top-region sprites culled/mis-positioned + flicker. Tier-1 `references/fact-sheets/Yamaha V9958 VDP.md` §6 line 120: "sprite data for line N is fetched during line N−1" (per-scanline check); §7 line 126 / §10 line 178: R#23 is a live per-line offset. Tier-2 corroboration (effect only, NEVER copy code): openMSX `SpriteChecker::sync()/checkUntil()` checks incrementally; each sprite-register write in `VDP.cc` syncs sprites to the current raster with the OLD value THEN applies the new — the SAME sync-before-change protocol our background already has.
  - **What M49 does (4 slices):** **S1** — a stateful `SpriteEngine::check_until(line)` watermark pass (mirroring `VdpScanlineAccumulator`, `vdp_scanline_accumulator.h:61-145`) that populates the per-line visible-sprite buffer + 5th-sprite reading `control_regs`+VRAM AT that raster point, replacing the single `recompute_frame()` sweep; per-line formulas + mode-2 base-mask + planar addressing preserved VERBATIM (only WHEN/with-WHAT-state changes; the R#1 BL / R#8 SPD / mode-0 gates become per-line-live). **S2** — drive it from the EXISTING M32 seam: on a sprite-relevant write (R#1/R#5/R#6/R#8/R#11/R#23 or sprite-attr VRAM) call sprite `check_until(line + 2)` with the SAME +2 boundary + the M44 watermark-direction discipline (`hbf1xv_machine.cpp:118-123`) so the sprite split lands on the identical line as the background; finalize + roll at `on_vsync()`. **S3** — feed the DEC-0031 line-granular collision / 5th-sprite / S#0 / S#3-S#6 machinery (`sprite_engine.cpp:238-325`) from the progressive pass, BYTE-IDENTICAL (D9 requires it). **S4** — keep R#23 in the sprite Y formula, per-line-LIVE (NOT removed); confirm direction via openMSX A/B on Space Manbow.
  - **Rule note:** this is an ALGORITHM change (WHEN/with-WHAT-state), NOT a data table — the D4/C1 license-sensitive-TABLE ban does NOT apply; the standing "never copy openMSX code" rule DOES (read `SpriteChecker` for effect only).
  - **Evidence gates (MANDATORY, HIGH blast radius):** build (both exes) + FULL ctest (every existing sprite/M22/M32 oracle UNMODIFIED + new M49 oracles); the FULL 13-mode 0.000% screen-mode A/B vs openMSX; Space Manbow + Laydock 2 headless before/after frame-capture verification (+ Space Manbow openMSX R#23-direction A/B) under `debug/m49/`; a DEC-0031 collision-byte-identity gate; determinism frame-hash equality. ZEXALL NOT required (zero cpu/core diff expected). Ban-attestation grep of `src/`.
  - **Residual risk (honest ceiling):** M49 removes the end-of-frame SNAPSHOT lag, bringing sprites to the background's per-line-live behavior with the SAME +2 line-granular rounding — it does NOT achieve cycle-exact intra-line splits (that needs the banned VDP access-slot position table, C1/D4 UNBUILDABLE-WITHOUT-FABRICATION). Cycle-timed intra-line cases like Aleste 2 stay LINE-quantized, the human-accepted M44 Phase 2b boundary (DEC-0069-OUTCOME). **Open sub-question:** whether Laydock 2's scoreboard "noise" is PURELY the sprite defect or ALSO a background facet — MUST be answered by a Laydock 2 repro during dev; a background facet, if found, is a SEPARATE new backlog row, NOT an M49 scope expansion.

Backlog D9 → in-progress (closes on M49 QA sign-off + human release). NOTE (coordinator to reconcile, independent of M49): `v9958_vdp.h:284-315` already references M48 Slice 1/2 access-timing seams while `current-phase.md` still labels M48 PLANNING — a state/code drift outside this planning cycle's evidence.
- Effective Date: 2026-07-14

  - **EXTERNALIZE to `sony_msx_hbf1xv.xml`:** (A) CLI-option/session defaults — main RAM KB (`--ram`), fast-disk, FM-PAC auto-load + slot, border, disk-writable, speed (0..7), and the SDL3-presentation knobs scale/filter/persistence/persistence-mode/fullscreen/capture (each an existing knob whose default is hardcoded in the M46 `resolve_session_defaults()` layer / `Sdl3AppConfig` struct); (B) machine sizing/paths — main RAM KB, VRAM KB, ROM/BIOS directory + the 7 BIOS ROM filenames (`f1xvbios/ext/kdr/disk/mus/kfn/firm.rom`, `hbf1xv_machine.cpp:513-520`), FM-PAC ROM + SRAM path, softwaredb path; slot layout as an OPTIONAL validated-to-builtin echo.
  - **HARD-EXCLUDE (stay hardcoded — the immutable silicon spec, reference-precedence tier 1; a bad XML edit must NEVER be able to break accuracy):** Z80A 3.58 MHz clock + frame-cycle constants, IM1=13T/IM2=19T/NMI=11T interrupt-ack (DEC-0074), S1985 +1 M1 wait, V9958 154/88/31 access slots + 1368 cyc/line + the M48/M49-era parity values, WD2793 FDC cycle constants. Evidence gate: empty `git diff` over `src/core`, `src/devices/cpu`, `src/devices/video/vdp_access_timing.h`, `src/devices/video/{v9958_vdp,sprite_engine}.*`, `src/devices/fdc/wd2793.cpp`, `src/devices/chipset/s1985_engine.*`.
  - **Precedence:** explicit CLI arg > XML value > built-in default (per knob, resolved in the M46 anti-drift Layer-B CLI-resolution seam; the machine ctor `kDramBytes` + `Sdl3AppConfig`/`ParsedSdl3Cli` stock defaults stay UNCHANGED).
  - **Missing/malformed (graceful — DECIDED):** file-not-found → ONE WARNING + built-in defaults, continue; a bad VALUE (unknown key / wrong type / out-of-range) → per-key WARNING naming the key + fall back to THAT key's default, the rest of the file still applying; a structurally-broken file → one WARNING + whole-file fallback. Never crash, never partial-apply.
  - **Determinism guard (CRITICAL — keeps the ~235-test suite byte-identical):** `config.xml` auto-loads ONLY in a genuinely interactive SDL3 launch (WITHOUT `--hidden-window`); the headless exe NEVER auto-loads (default scaffold, `--debug-session`, all `*-parity` modes); SDL3 `--hidden-window` (test/CI) does NOT auto-load; `--config <path>` is the explicit opt-in that forces load in any mode (no test passes it). Search order (interactive SDL3): `--config` → exe-dir → CWD, first-found-wins.
  - **Reuse the existing XML machinery:** extract the tolerant `TagScanner` tokenizer from `src/machine/software_db.cpp:37-136` into a shared `src/machine/xml_tokenizer.*` (behavior-preserving; software-db tests are the guard) + a new `src/machine/emulator_config.*` model/validator; NO new third-party XML dependency.
  - **Shipped reference:** a TRACKED, fully-commented `sony_msx_hbf1xv.xml` at repo root (verified not gitignored) with every knob + default + allowed range; its values equal the built-in defaults so ship+load-unedited == no-config (round-trip identity).
  - **Slices:** S1 config model + strict parser/validator (reuse the XML reader) · S2 CLI-default resolution wiring (CLI>XML>default precedence + the determinism rule + `--config`) · S3 machine-config sizing/paths (BIOS dir + 7 filenames + FM-PAC/softwaredb paths + RAM KB; VRAM validated-to-128; slots validated-to-builtin) · S4 shipped reference config + docs + round-trip test.
  - **Evidence gates:** validate-assets, checksum, build (both exes), full ctest (baseline count + new config unit/round-trip/precedence/fallback/determinism tests, pre-M50 tests byte-identical), the §3 empty-diff accuracy gate. openMSX A/B NOT required (pure config plumbing; every settable value was already A/B-validated in its origin milestone — RAM M42, FM-PAC/fast-disk M46, video/persistence M37/M39; the timing-constant diff is empty). ZEXALL NOT run (zero cpu/core diff).
- Impacted Milestones: **M50 (opens, PLANNING).** Expected edits confined to `src/machine/{emulator_config,xml_tokenizer,software_db}.*`, `src/machine/hbf1xv_machine.cpp` (asset-path resolution), `src/frontend/{sdl3_cli,sdl3_main}.*`, `src/main.cpp` (`--debug-session` + `--config`), new tests, and the root `sony_msx_hbf1xv.xml`. ZERO `src/core`, ZERO `src/devices/cpu`, ZERO timing constants → NORMAL human-release gate (no auto-close). No new backlog rows (M50 is production hardening, not a deferred-scope item).
- Risk Notes: R1 determinism perturbation (mitigated by the airtight auto-load gating); R2 precedence/anti-drift bugs; R3 malformed-input robustness; R4 accuracy leak (mitigated by the HARD-EXCLUDE + empty-diff gate + VRAM-128/slots-builtin validation); R5 software_db refactor regression (guarded by its tests). All values the XML can set are pre-existing, individually-validated knobs; M50 changes only WHERE the default comes from, never WHAT a value does.

- Decision ID: DEC-0078
- Requested By: Human (project owner, source of truth), 2026-07-15 — CRITICAL live-play defect report, gameplay-breaking ("completely making the gameplay unplayable"). Owner pre-authorized a FULLY AUTONOMOUS coordinator run: no human questions, best-judgement decisions delegated, plan→build→test until resolved.
- Approved By: MSX Master Agent (coordinator). Opens **M51** in the PLANNING phase (planner-first). Universal, spec-modeling fix only (never game-specific), under the reference-precedence directive (DEC-0073).
- Decision: **Open M51 — root-cause and fix the sprite disappearance/flicker-during-scroll defect (post-M49 sprite-subsystem regression or residual).**
  - **Defect (three independent live repros, all KonamiSCC carts on v1.2.0-era builds):** (1) **Aleste 2** (`games/roms/Aleste 2/aleste2.rom`, launched `--bios-dir bios/ --slot1 ... --disk-writable`, otherwise convenience defaults incl. 512 KB modded RAM + FM-PAC slot 2): the player's plane sprite completely DISAPPEARS and RE-APPEARS as the game scrolls. (2) **Laydock 2** (disk): same disappearance symptom per the owner. (3) **Firebird / Hi no Tori Hououhen** (`games/roms/firebird/firebird.rom`): the player character flickers CONSTANTLY and flying enemy sets flicker "like hell", while ground-locked objects that move with the scrolling ground do NOT flicker — a clean sprite-layer vs background-layer discriminator (background rendering is healthy; the sprite subsystem is the defect locus).
  - **Timeline discipline:** the defect is being reported AFTER M48 (v1.1.5, access-slot contention = the owner's "adjustable VDP timing" suspicion) and M49 (v1.1.6, per-line-live sprite fetch, D9) both shipped. Candidate attributions — (a) an M49 regression in the per-line-live watermark/segment discipline (e.g., per-line visible-sprite buffer accumulation/clearing across mid-frame `check_until` segments, 5th/8-sprite-limit misfiring, segment boundary quantization moving frame-to-frame), (b) an M48 timing-overlay interaction shifting WHEN game ISR writes land relative to sprite segments, (c) the honestly-documented M49 residual (1-frame-lag + cycle-timed intra-line ceiling) now proving gameplay-breaking, (d) a distinct latent sprite/R#23 defect. **All four are HYPOTHESES — none is pre-decided; the developer must attribute by evidence.**
  - **Coordinator recon (evidence so far, hypothesis-grade):** `src/devices/video/sprite_engine.cpp:263-267` sprite-line formula `((line-1) + r23 - y) & 0xFF` MATCHES openMSX `SpriteChecker.cc:104-127` (`displayDelta = verticalScroll - lineZero`; `spriteLine = (displayLine - y) & 0xFF`) including R#23 participation and the checked-one-line-earlier convention; mode-2 sentinel 216 matches. So the STATIC formula is at tier-2 parity — suspicion falls on the DYNAMIC path (M49 `check_until` watermark, per-line buffer lifecycle, seam-driven segment splits, M48 timing shifts).
  - **Decisive tools available:** deterministic `--input-script`/`--dump-frame` repro; **git bisect across v1.1.4 (pre-M48) → v1.1.5 (M48) → v1.1.6 (M49) → v1.2.0** with the same script+frame-hash oracle to pin the regressing milestone; per-frame sprite-presence analysis over consecutive frame dumps (flicker = sprite present/absent alternation); openMSX A/B on the identical inputs.
  - **Blast radius: HIGH** (all sprite rendering, all 13 modes) → NORMAL human-release gate, NO auto-close; the fix itself must keep the DEC-0031 collision byte-identity and every existing sprite/M22/M32/M49 oracle green (or honestly re-derive with justification, never weaken).
  - **Evidence gates (mandatory):** clean build both exes; full fast-subset ctest; 13-mode 0.000% screen A/B vs openMSX; DEC-0031 collision-byte-identity; before/after deterministic frame captures for Aleste 2 + Firebird (+ Laydock 2 if disk repro is workable) under `debug/m51/`; ZEXALL only if `src/devices/cpu`/`src/core` are touched (not expected).
- Impacted Milestones: **M51 (opens, PLANNING).** Expected edits confined to `src/devices/video/{sprite_engine,v9958_vdp}.*` + possibly `src/machine/hbf1xv_machine.cpp` (seam); ZERO `src/core`, ZERO `src/devices/cpu` expected. Backlog D9 disposition may be amended by findings (M49 closed it; if M51 proves an M49 regression the fix REPAIRS D9's closure rather than reopening scope).

Owner-acknowledged consequence: game `.dsk` images are mutated by default (arguably MORE authentic — a real MSX writes its floppies); `--no-disk-writable` is the escape hatch.

- Decision ID: DEC-0080
- Requested By: Human (project owner, source of truth), 2026-07-15 — new standalone tool request: "i added a folder called diskutils. within that I want a single executable that creates MSX disk. msx-disk.exe --create | --read (shows the content of the disk in HEX) | --format (format the disk that's fully compatible with this MSX2+)". Followed by an explicit STRUCTURE DIRECTIVE: "the source code of the diskutil must be under 'src/' and compiled binary should exist in diskutils/".
- Approved By: MSX Master Agent (coordinator), after msx-orchestration follow-up gate validation PASS (2026-07-15: M52 terminally closed, no dangling obligations, next base decision = DEC-0080). Opens **M53** in the PLANNING phase (planner-first).
- Decision: **Open M53 — standalone MSX disk utility `msx-disk.exe` — AND ratify the new scope area.**
  - **Scope-area ratification (guardrails: scope changes need a decision):** the repository layout gains (a) `src/diskutils/` — host-side disk-utility source (a NEW src responsibility line to be added to `src/CLAUDE.md`; boundary rule: no emulator machine/device logic leaks in, and the emulator never depends on `src/diskutils/`), and (b) `diskutils/` (owner-created, verified empty + not gitignored) — the build-output home of the compiled `msx-disk.exe` (post-build copy from the ONE `build/` tree; DEC-0041 single-build-tree policy intact). Default disposition, pending owner preference: the SOURCE is tracked; the compiled `diskutils/msx-disk.exe` binary is gitignored (repo convention — build products are not committed); owner may override to track the binary.
  - **Tool contract (planner refines):** one executable, three modes — `--create` (produce a new, fully-formatted blank 720 KB `.dsk` image), `--read` (hex dump of disk content to stdout), `--format` (re-format an existing image in place). Output MUST be fully compatible with THIS machine (HB-F1XV MSX2+ / WD2793 / Sony Disk ROM): 720 KB 3.5" DD geometry — 80 tracks × 2 sides × 9 sectors/track × 512 B/sector — MSX-DOS FAT12 layout with a correct MSX boot sector. Grounding: the repo's own `DiskImage` code, `tools/format-blank-disk.ps1` (M36 S-c prior art), the real `disks/` MSX-DOS images as oracles, and reference materials per DEC-0073 precedence (cite concrete paths).
  - **Isolation (CRITICAL):** additive CMake target only; the emulator's 247/247 deterministic suite must stay byte-identical; reuse of internal disk-image knowledge must not couple emulator behavior to the tool.
  - **Evidence gates:** build (emulator both exes + new target); full fast-subset ctest unchanged + new tool tests (create/read/format round-trips, boot-sector/FAT oracles); an integration cross-check that a `--create`/`--format` image MOUNTS AND BOOTS DISK BASIC / is accepted by the emulator's own FDC headlessly; validate-assets + checksum unchanged. openMSX A/B N/A (host-side file utility, no device behavior). ZEXALL N/A (zero cpu/core).
- Impacted Milestones: **M53 (opens, PLANNING).** Expected edits: NEW `src/diskutils/*`, `CMakeLists.txt` wiring, `src/CLAUDE.md` responsibility line, `.gitignore` (binary), `tests/` additions, README/docs. ZERO `src/core`, `src/devices`, `src/machine`, `src/frontend` behavior changes. LOW blast radius (isolated target) → NORMAL human-release gate (owner user-test), no auto-close.
- Risk Notes: R1 suite perturbation via CMake/global-flag side effects (mitigate: additive target + full ctest byte-identity gate); R2 wrong FAT12/boot-sector layout (mitigate: oracle vs real msxdos23.dsk + emulator boot cross-check); R3 in-place `--format` data destruction (mitigate: planner defines overwrite/confirmation semantics); R4 scope creep into emulator internals (mitigate: dependency direction rule in this decision).
- Effective Date: 2026-07-15

- Decision ID: DEC-0081
- Requested By: Human (project owner, source of truth), 2026-07-15 — "is this possible to add macOS support ... i have a macOS machine. let's only do thorough planning. then i will git down the code on my mac and continue from there. once again, this must compile on both machines. keeping that in mind that i do not intend to separate the repo. i want have single codebase, and that we can build to target machine (best is auto-detect at build time)."
- Approved By: MSX Master Agent (coordinator), after msx-orchestration gate validation PASS (2026-07-15, third validation; planning-only closure confirmed protocol-compliant — developer/QA gates DEFERRED to the owner's macOS-side continuation, not skipped; M54 stays OPEN).
- Decision: **Open M54 — macOS support (single codebase, dual-toolchain), PLANNING-ONLY THIS CYCLE.**
  - **Hard requirements (owner):** ONE repo, ONE codebase — no fork, no platform branches; the same tree must compile on Windows (MSVC) AND macOS (AppleClang); the target platform is auto-detected at build time (CMake toolchain/platform detection — `if(MSVC)`/`if(WIN32)`/`if(APPLE)` branching only, no separate build files).
  - **Coordinator recon (grounded):** src/ has ZERO Win32 API usage (no windows.h/_WIN32/__declspec), `CMAKE_CXX_EXTENSIONS OFF`, MSVC-/WIN32-only build bits already guarded (`CMakeLists.txt:29` /utf-8, `:161` DLL staging, `:188` icon .rc), no backslash/drive-letter paths in src/, tests are pure C++ executables (no PowerShell inside ctest), SDL3 vendored with native macOS support (Metal/CoreAudio), both platforms little-endian (golden fixtures/hashes expected to carry over).
  - **This cycle delivers PLANNING ONLY:** `docs/m54-planner-package.md` — portability audit surface with concrete file:line, CMake platform-matrix design, line-ending/.gitattributes policy decision (CRLF/LF mixing observed — text-mode fixture reads are a determinism risk), filename-case audit, tooling strategy (tools/*.ps1 under pwsh vs portable equivalents; openMSX A/B natively on macOS — no WSL), single-config generator handling, macOS packaging non-goals (plain binary this milestone; .app/.icns polish deferred), macOS-side acceptance criteria (AppleClang clean build of all 3 targets: headless, sdl3, msx-disk; full fast ctest parity to the Windows 253 baseline; determinism byte-identity checks), risks, and a step-by-step MACOS RUNBOOK the owner executes on their Mac (clone → prerequisites → configure → build → ctest → evidence capture → troubleshooting).
  - **Anti-fabrication constraint (decisive):** macOS build/test evidence CANNOT be produced on this Windows machine; the developer gate is blocked on real macOS hardware (owner-owned). NO REQ-M54-002 developer handoff is issued this cycle. When the owner continues on the Mac, the normal developer-evidence → QA-signoff ordering resumes there.
- Impacted Milestones: **M54 (opens, PLANNING; stays OPEN at cycle end).** Expected eventual edit locus (Mac-side): CMakeLists platform branches, possible mechanical #include fixes surfaced by AppleClang, .gitattributes, README/docs, tools portability shims. ZERO device/timing behavior expected → openMSX A/B N/A; ZEXALL only if a shim ever touches src/core|src/devices/cpu (scope to avoid). Blast radius LOW-MED (build system) → NORMAL human-release gate.
- Risk Notes (headline; full set in the package): R1 AppleClang strictness / missing transitive includes; R2 line-ending-induced fixture divergence (needs .gitattributes decision); R3 SDL3Config discovery on the Mac prefix path; R4 case-sensitive-filesystem asset-name traps; R5 PowerShell tooling gap on macOS; R6 single-vs-multi-config ctest invocation differences.
- Effective Date: 2026-07-15

- Decision ID: DEC-0082
- Requested By: Human (project owner, source of truth), 2026-07-16 — "the agents on the macOS cannot see the doc and references as well as the agent files as they are not pushed on github. lets push them so two can communicate. … you can push the docs and references, claude agent files, etc so that you two are completely bi-directional via github."
- Approved By: Coordinator (main session), executing the owner's explicit direction. This REVERSES the 2026-07-10 local-only carve-out (.gitignore "Local-only development apparatus" block) and restores the DEC-0047 whole-repo-as-single-source-of-truth posture, now motivated by the dual-machine (Windows + macOS) workflow: git is the ONLY carrier between the two machines, and the M54 cycle proved the gitignored trees cannot coordinate cross-machine work.
- Decision: **Publish the development apparatus — track and push `docs/`, `references/`, `.claude/` (minus settings.local.json), `agent-protocol/`, `tests/`, `tools/`, root `CLAUDE.md`, `src/CLAUDE.md` (and tests/CLAUDE.md via tests/).**
  - **Stays ignored:** `build/` (regenerable), `debug/` (regenerable runtime captures; existing `!` evidence exceptions unchanged), `games/` (game library, never tracked), `roms/`/`disks/` content policy unchanged (DEC-0047-AMENDMENT-B/C), `.claude/settings.local.json` (per-machine by Claude Code convention), editor cruft.
  - **Licensing disclosure (references/, recorded honestly — the owner's DEC-0047 accepted-risk posture extends here):** `references/openmsx-21.0/` (GPL v2 — unmodified source redistribution permitted with license text retained, present in-tree); `references/sdl3/` (zlib — redistribution permitted); `references/zexall/` (GPL v2 — permitted); `references/fact-sheets/` + curated docs (project-authored); `references/fmsx-60/` (Marat Fayzullin's fMSX 6.0 — per the project's recorded understanding "freeware, NON-COMMERCIAL DISTRIBUTION ONLY, not open-source"; publishing on this non-commercial public repo is distribution under that non-commercial allowance, and its bundled executables/generic MSX ROMs ride along — the SAME accepted-risk category as the DEC-0047 bios/ decision; NO redistribution rights are asserted, no provenance claim is made, and the owner may direct removal at any time). The GPL trees' license files publish with them; the repo's own license notice (personal/non-commercial reference) is compatible with this posture.
  - **Size impact:** ~85 MB / ~5,200 files added to the remote (references/ = 74.9 MB / 4,636 files dominant).
  - **Cross-machine reconciliation protocol (one-time, Mac side):** the Mac's local untracked copies of these trees will COLLIDE with the pulled tracked versions (git refuses to overwrite untracked files). The Mac session must: (1) move its local `agent-protocol/`, `docs/`, `.claude/`, `tests/`, `tools/`, `references/`, `CLAUDE.md`, `src/CLAUDE.md` aside (e.g. `mv X X.macside`), (2) `git pull`, (3) reconcile — append any Mac-side-only ledger entries (its M54 REQ/RESP records) into the now-tracked `agent-protocol/` channels as an append-only merge, verify its docs (m54 evidence artifacts) are represented, then delete the `.macside` copies. From then on BOTH machines commit/push/pull these trees normally — append-only channel discipline is now enforced across machines via git merge behavior (concurrent appends to the same channel file merge cleanly or conflict visibly; the ISO-8601-timestamped entry format keeps ordering auditable).
- Impacted Milestones: none functionally (repo policy). The protocol ledger, planner packages, QA sign-offs, agents, tests, and tools become the shared cross-machine source of truth.
- Effective Date: 2026-07-16
